like, this simple rinky dink little shit works

```
A = 2
D = A
A = 0x7FFF

*A = 1
*A = D

*A = 1
*A = D

*A = 1
*A = D

```


but this, glorious loop that remembers the previous state of the lamp and lets you choose any number of blinks, doesn't

```
# Assembler code 
# reset values
# 0 is for loop counter
A = 0
*A = 0
# 1 is for light tracker
A = 1
*A = 0
# if light was on, jump to OFF
A = 1
D = *A
A = 12
D - 1;JEQ
# turn light ON & APPLY
A = 1
*A = 1
A = 16
A;JMP
# turn light OFF & APPLY
A = 2
D = A
A = 1
*A = D
# APPLY new value
A = 1
D = *A
A = 0x7FFF
*A = D
# next loop
A = 0
*A = *A + 1
A = 200
D = A
A = 0
D = *A - D
A = 4
D;JlT
```
